CHARACTER SETUP and Creation: *[roll or calc wil be used for CALCULATION]

										Attributes-> Derived From Stats [Base Attributes/Normal character = 5][All charcters]

	-Strength = how strong the character is
		Tied to Torso, Arm and Legs.
          [Torso = 50% of strength stat]
          [Arms = 10% of strength stat each]
          [Legs = 15% of strength stat]
         	= Power 40%,  Stamina 40%, Toughness 20%
	-Intelligence = how smart the character  is/ How many logcial steps the character can navigate
		Tied to Head[50%] and Internal [stomach[25%] & brain[25%]]
		= Charisma 10%, Muscle Memory 20%, Aptitude 70%
	-Endurance = how much energy the character has
		Tied to Internal [lungs[33%], muscle[33%], and fat[33%]]
		= Stamina 50%, Quickness 15%, Muscle Memory 15%, Constution 20%
	-Dexterity = How well the charcter moves and performs fine /or fluid motions
		Tied to Hands[50%] and Internal [eyes[50%]]
		= Accuracy 50%, Quickness 25%, Muscle Memory 25%
	-Willpower = How mentally and physically tough the character is
		Tied to Internal [brain]
		= Toughness 25%, Resilience 25%, Aptitude 20%, Constitution 30%
	-Perception = How acute is the characters sense are
		Tied to Internal [Eyes[25%], Ears[25%], Nose[25%], Skin[25%]]
	 	= Accuracy 50%, Charisma 20%, Resilience 15%, Aptitude 15%

	Height (in cm) = used for metabolism and body comp calculations

	*If linked body part takes damage stat is reduced by [.1 x Dmg]. Attributes are wieghted by associated stat instead of being directly leveled, making both manage through skill leveling.

		-Stats = [Attribute/10]- Derived From Skills ->Skills set on character creation/Npc skills generated with Job [Job*on Social Sim Page]

	[Strength + Dexterity] = Power <- How much force the character generates [Combat Stats -  Power 17%, Agriculture Stats- Power 30%, Stoneworking Stats-  Power 30%, Athletics Stats-  Power 20%, Metallurgy Stats- Power 22.5%,]
	[Perception + Dexterity] = Accuracy <- Charcters hand eye coordination skill [Combat Stats - Accuracy 17%, Survival Stats- Accuracy 25%, Stoneworking Stats- Accuracy 30%, Roguery Stats- Accuracy 35%, Athletics Stats-  Accuracy 20%, Artistry Stats - Accuracy 40%,]
	[Perception + Intellingence] = Charisma <- Characters social awareness [Roguery Stats- Charisma 35%, Speech Stats - Charisma 50%, Athletics Stats- 10%]
	[Strength + Endurance] = Stamina <- The amount of energy a character can exert at once [Combat Stats -  Stamina 16.5%, Survival Stats-  Stamina 25%, Agriculture Stats- Stamina 40%, Stoneworking Stats- Stamina 40%, Athletics Stats- Stamina 20%, Metallurgy Stats- Stamina 22.5%, Artistry Stats - Stamina 10%]
	[Willpower + Strength] = Toughness <- How much damage a characters body can absorb [Combat Stats - Toughness 16.5%, Survival Stats-  Toughness 25%, Agriculture Stats- Toughness 20%, Metallurgy Stats- Toughness 22.5%,]
	[Dexterity + Endurance] = Quickness <- How well the character can navigate spacial movement (proprioception) [Combat Stats - Quickness 16.5%, Athletics Stats-  Quickness 20%,] 
	[Willpower + Percpetion] = Resilience <- How well the character can guard against mental attacks &/or recover from them. [Survival Stats-  Resilience 25%, Athletics Stats- Resilience 10%, Metallurgy Stats- Resilience 22.5%]
	[Intelligence + Endurance + Dexterity]/1.5 = Muscle Memory <- Governs skill retention and potential [Combat Stats - Muscle Memory 16.5%, Agriculture Stats- Muscle Memory 10%, Athletics Stats- Muscle Memory 10%, Metallurgy Stats- Muscle Memory 10%,]
	[Intelligence + Willpower + Perception]/1.5 = Aptitude <- How well the character can learn a skill, execute, and or strategize [Governs Exp gain. [Natural Skill](Cannot be trained)] [Roguery Stats- Aptitude 30%, Learning Stats - Aptitude 100%, Artistry Stats - Aptitude 50%, Speech Stats - Aptitude 50%]
	[Willpower + Endurance] = Constitution/Lifeforce [Qi/Ki/Chakra] <- Represents the characters pysche and body (soul). [Control Stats - Constitution 90%, Survival - 10% ] 

	[Point distr.- stats range 1-100, an avg character is 50 in all stat categories, 5 in all attributes]

	Limb Integrity (Links Limb/Total Health, Lifeforce, Chakra Points, & Meridians-> Calculates Pain lvls) = [[BodyPart-Hp% (x)(char)Mass(total)]*[[(BodyPart-Organ)(x)(Organ Weight Distribution %)] x Tissue kcal Distribution]
														= The Amount of kcals currently contained in a limb. Damage to limbs must be repaired with kcals. 
	Track Body Parts													Buffing Limbs requires kcals. The Force of internal effects are resisted in kcals
	Limb Integrity = The kcal of specific body parts
	Current Limb Integrity = The kcal of specific body parts
	Max Limb Integrity = Maximum instanstaneous kcal injection a limb can withstand before energy of change must be resisted with Will.= [Limb Integrity + 3,500] x Limb Skill
	Chakra Points = Qi is Aether as kcals that is controlled by Chakra Points (Hearts) and Meridians/Leylines (Arteries/Veins). Each Chakra Point contains the kcals of its associated limb.
			= [Cumulative Max Limb/Organ Integrity], Meaning Earth = Earth + Metal + Wood = Root [Starting size/stats = Organs/Chakra Points]

					.			Body and Chakra Points Diagram [for flow Chakra points listed first]

	This diagram visualizes how the Core elements anchor to the primary energy centers, with Branch offshoots radiating from their parent nodes.
	
	Root (Red): Earth anchors here, branching into Metal (structural) and Wood (flexible).
	Sacral (Orange): Water anchors here, feedinsg the compound Ice.
	Solar Plexus (Yellow): Fire anchors here, sparking the compound Lightning.
	Heart (Green): Air anchors here, providing the motion for Lightning and the temperature for Ice.

								The Unified Elemental Chart - 

			This chart explains how each element manifests within the body's energy centers and its specific biological function.

	Element Type		Element	Description/Origin						Primary Chakra				Body Relation

	Core	Earth		The stabilizing foundation for all physical matter.			Root (Muladhara)		Skeletal system, spine, (solid tissues). (All Organs)
	Branch	Metal		Earth + Fire + Air: The refined, mineral essence of the earth.		Root (Sub-point)		Teeth, bone marrow, and mineral absorption. (Bones)
	Branch	Wood		Earth + Water + Air: The organic, living extension of the earth.	Root (Sub-point)		Muscles, tendons, and cellular growth.  (Muscle Group)
	Core	Water		The fluid force of change and circulation.				Sacral (Svadhisthana)		Kidneys, bladder, and reproductive fluids. (Vitals)
	Core	Fire		The metabolic energy and transformative heat.				Solar Plexus (Manipura)		Digestive system and metabolic "fire". (Heart,Stomach, Lungs)
	Core	Air		The movement and life-breath (Prana).					Heart (Anahata)			Respiratory system and circulation of oxygen. (Heart, Lungs)
	Branch	Lightning	Fire + Air + Water: High-frequency energy discharge.		        Solar Plexus / Heart		Nervous system and electrical impulses in the brain.(Skin, Muscle, Brain, Eyes, Nose, Spine)
	Branch	Ice		Water + Air + Earth : Solidified fluid via thermal loss.		Sacral / Root	                Temperature regulation and joint preservation.(Arteries & Veins)



		Brain & Psyche/Senses- Psyche & Sense connect to brain for mental attacks and sense-reliabity, Qi and Pysche sense. Tri-Nature Point activation can be activated on brain to (+)raise or (-)lower associted sense. 1 sense point = 3,500 kcals](see magic system)
		Senses-		Stimuli-
	 	1. Sight    	Light
  		2. Smell        Odarants [Chemical Molecules/compounds] #{Enum is same as Flavors}
		3. Hearing 	Sound #{Verb type}
		4. Touch	Pressure #{Feelings:{adjective type} [Weight/Pressure- Heavy- Moderately/Extremely, Light- Moderately/Extremely ], [Hardness- Hard/Soft],[Sharpness- Sharp/Pointed/Blunt] }
		5. Taste        [Chemical Molecules/compounds] #{Flavors Enum}
		6. Temperature	Radiation/Heat [Though temperature is exprienced through touch, this will be split for Body-Sense purposes]
		7. ESP		[Psychic sense] = [Sense Hp [1-7] = Constitution + Resilience]
		8. Rationale	[Emotional State = Logos, Pathos, Ethos][Hp = [Skill lvl x Learning skill]reprsented as(50 -> range from 0 [+/-])(+/-)]
		9. Morale       [Couragessness + Confidence][Both bars work in tandem Couragessness rise +1 with every "Sucessfull action", and +1 for "Positive interactions". "Negative interactions" inflicts -4 dmg per event on Couragessness.
								For every +2 Couragessness earns gain +1 Confidence. "Action Failure" inflicts -4 dmg per event on Confidence. Confidence Homeostasis inactive until Courage is atleast 0 if +]
									Food Score is directly applied here.
"Sucessfull action" -> Action = Expected outcome -> ex. Crafting Success, Dmg Dealt, Trade made
"Positive interactions"-> Positive Speech Dmg
"Negative interactions" -> Negative Speech Dmg
"Action Failure" -> Action ≠ Expected outcome -> Player sets crafting timer to end before craft finishes= quitting, Missed attacks, Taking Dmg, Failed trades
"Craft-Timer" -> Time player expects it takes to craft 1 of selected item at current skill lvl
			Crafting cant't be failed Timer is estimated timeto craft vs Actual. Success state on first try x2's item quality. Subsequent tries lower base quality .1 per try.

	[Sense & Rationale Tracking - e.states "hp" starts at 0, + attack raise hp, - attacks lower hp. Applies to both speech and mental attacks.}		

	ESP & Sense- Esp Represents the sense of imagine/percieve reality and the mental link between the two (The ability of the mind to influence imagined/perceived reality).
			Senses 1-6 - Follow Rationale logic for damage and simulation. Sense 7 [ESP] - is the only sense with proper "hp" score. "Attacks" + or -.
			Mental Attack calc = Spell effect dmg - Enemy-Resilience = Pen check-> Pen-check - ESP = Mental dmg taken [MDT] -> MDT x 10 = Damage to targeted Sense
			Speech combat does not effect ESP or Sense.
    
		For short-hand design mental attack will use Pysche targeting in the same way physical attacks use bodypart targeting [Since touch is a physical sense it will target a bodypart but will damage the sense]
		Psyche-Damage - Senses cannot be mentally destroyed; therefore won't lose or gain health. Rather each sense has a Tolerance level that functions as health. When Stimulated the current Tolerance is raised,
				If max tolerance is exceeded that sense is overrwhelemed and becomes unreliable. When Deprived the current Tolerance is decreased, if min Tolerance is exceeded that sense is dimmed or disabled.

		[Sense & Rationale Tracking]
		Baseline: 0 (Homeostatic Set-Point)
		Attack Range: [+] raise HP (Over-stimulation/Mania), [-] lower HP (Deprivation/Depression)
		Manual Override: Tri-Nature Point activation [+/-] 1 Sense Point = 3,500 kcals

		[The Drift: Recovery Calculation]
		Sense Drift (1-7):
    			Drift = MAX (1,|CurrentHP|/(Constitution + Resilience)) × (1/(1 + Exposure_Turns/9,000))
		
		Rationale Drift (8):
    			Drift = MAX (5,|CurrentHP|/Skill-Lvl) × (1/(1 + Exposure_Turns/9,000))
    		(Rationale HP recovers toward 0 at a rate dictated by Logos/Pathos/Ethos proficiency)

		[Senses- Stimuli- Recovery Constants]
		1. Sight      (Light)          [Normal. Constant: 300 turns (Fast) / 9,000 (Deep)]
		2. Smell      (Odorants)       [Normal. Constant: 9,000 turns]
		3. Hearing    (Sound)          [Normal. Constant: 300 turns (Fast) / 9,000 (Deep)]
		4. Touch      (Pressure)       [Normal. Constant: 9,000 turns]
		5. Taste      (Chemicals)      [Normal. Constant: 9,000 turns]
		6. Temp       (Radiation)      [Normal. Constant: 9,000 turns]
		7. ESP        (Psychic)        [Normal. Constant: 9,000 turns]
		8. Rationale  (E.States)       [Normal. Constant: 9,000 turns]
		9. Morale     (2C.States)      [Normal. Constant: 9,000 turns]

		[Rationale State Mechanics]
		HP Range: [-50 < 0 > +50]
		Mental Attack: (Speech/Psyche) moves HP away from 0.
		Homeostasis: Passive Drift pulls HP back to 0 (The Neutral Mind).


			 [Fatigue = intensity and duration of anaerobic effort. If Fatigue = Max Stamina character has 100% chance to become immobile/comatose.
					Fatigue Accumulation: Fatigue increases faster when HR exceeds the character’s Aerobic Threshold (75% MHR) and accelerates sharply past Anaerobic Threshold (85–90% MHR).
					Each 10% of max stamina burned still generates 1 fatigue point, but HR zone modifies the rate:
																	Zone 1–2 (<75% MHR): No modifier
																	Zone 3 (75–85% MHR): +25% fatigue rate
																	Zone 4 (85–90% MHR): +50% fatigue rate
																	Zone 5 (>90% MHR): +100% fatigue rate

	Vigor Points (VP) - [Constitution + Total Health + Stamina = The absolute health of the characters pysche and body (soul).] 
		    [Life Bar: represents the junction of Health, Stamina and Ki - Character action resource]
		    [Character Dies when depleted]
	            [Base recovery = .5 per tick] [HR‑Linked Vigor Stress: Sustained HR above Anaerobic Threshold increases VP strain.For every minute spent above 90% MHR, apply a VP tax equal to 1% of max VP.]
										[This represents systemic stress and oxygen debt.]

	Agility - [Quickness + Accuracy = Characters movement and attack speed [base value for avg character is 1.2 sec or 1 turn]
	Resistance - [Toughness + Resilience = Resistance against abstract damage; poison, burns, frost, hemmoraging]
	Hit-Chance/Evasion[Finesse] (Spatial Reasoning)(SR) - [([Accuracy] + [Agility]) x 0.01] Represents subtle body movements such as flinching, and fine motion accuracy 		
	Metabolism - [Influences HP,SP, And VP, Bodyweight, and Satiation/thirst Levels]
	     BaseMetabolic Burn Rate (BM_BR):
					BMR Calculation (Harris‑Benedict): baseline caloric requirement before activity multipliers.
					Men:𝐵𝑀𝑅= 88.362 + (13.397⋅𝑊)+ (4.799⋅𝐻) − (5.677⋅𝐴)
					Women:𝐵𝑀𝑅= 447.593 +(9.247⋅𝑊) +(3.098⋅𝐻) − (4.330⋅𝐴)
								Activity Multipliers:
									Sedentary = 1.2
									Light = 1.375
									Moderate = 1.55
									Heavy = 1.725
									Maximal = 1.9
						(Where (W) = weight in kg, (H) = height in cm, (A) = age). 
					[These multipliers apply only when HR‑based burn is not used.]	

 
	     Hunger - Current Satiation Level
	     Thirst - ""[Static water loss range inbetween 25mL to 37.5mL per hour, first stage of thirst begins in range 1% to 2% bodywater lost.
	     Calories - [Starting Weight (Total caloric makeup of the character body) = 21.5 x (Height x Height) ]
				[Cont. Weight = Internals + Fluids + MRV+ CRV ]

										Dynamic HR‑Based Caloric Burn:  
						Replace fixed activity burn rates with continuous HR‑derived caloric expenditure when HR data is available.

						Men: Calories/min = ( 0.6309𝐻𝑅 + 0.1988 𝑊 + 0.2017𝐴 − 55.0969)
										/4.184
						Women: Calories/min = ( 0.4472𝐻𝑅 − 0.1263 + 0.074𝐴 − 20.4022)
										/4.184
						If HR is not being tracked, fall back to the existing fixed activity categories.

						Dynamic Heart Rate Thresholds
						Maximum Heart Rate (MHR):𝑀𝐻𝑅=220-age
						Aerobic Threshold (AT):𝐴𝑇=0.75⋅𝑀𝐻𝑅
						Anaerobic Threshold (LT):𝐿𝑇=0.85–0.90⋅𝑀𝐻𝑅

						Stamina Burn Logic (HR‑Driven)
						HR Zone	%	MHR	Effect
						Zone 1		50–60%	Minimal stamina burn
						Zone 2		60–75%	Light stamina burn
						Zone 3		75–85%	Moderate stamina burn (+25% fatigue)
						Zone 4		85–90%	Heavy stamina burn (+50% fatigue)
						Zone 5		90–100%	Maximal burn (+100% fatigue, VP strain)

						Fatigue Logic (HR‑Driven)
							Fatigue accumulates based on HR zone rather than fixed activity categories.
							Fatigue prevents stamina regeneration as defined in the original system.

										Base Caloric burn rate - Sedentary 1 per minute/ approx .017 per sec/tick/turn
			 										 Light 3 per minute/ approx .051 per sec/tick/turn 330% 
			 										 Moderate 5 per minute/ approx .084 per sec/tick/turn/ 500% increase
                         										 Heavy 12 per minute/ approx .2 per sec/tick/turn 1200% increase

										Base Caloric return/movement rate - Sedentary 1 per minute/ approx .017 per sec/tick/turn
														    Light 3 per minute/ approx .051 per sec/tick/turn
														    Moderate = [BBR (5 per minute/ approx .084 per sec/tick/turn/ 20% increase) x 1.5]
                         											    Heavy 12 per minute/ approx .2 per sec/tick/turn 83% increase [BBR (5 per minute/ approx .084 per sec/tick/turn/ 20% increase) x 2]

			Respiratory Rate (RR):  RR is derived from HR using the Pulse‑Respiration Quotient (PRQ = HR/RR ≈ 4:1).
						If RR deviates from expected PRQ due to low Endurance or fatigue, apply penalties to Quickness and increase fatigue accumulation rate.
							RR Stress Effects:  
					If RR exceeds expected PRQ‑aligned value by more than 20%, apply: −10% Quickness, +15% fatigue accumulation, +5% stamina burn rate
				
					If RR is below expected PRQ (poor ventilation), apply: −10% Accuracy, −10% Power, +10% VP strain[loss]	
				[During player action] Activity level = self-select		
						Each activity level maps to:
						A % of MHR
						A caloric multiplier
						A stamina burn modifier
						Example mapping:
						Sedentary = 50–60% MHR
						Light = 60–70% MHR
						Moderate = 70–80% MHR
						Hard = 80–90% MHR
						Maximal = 90–100% MHR

								Weight Distribution- 
  
	Base Weight generation based on height = 21.5 (BMI(median avg)) x (Height x Height) [sample of starting cal distribution: 21.5 BMI x (176cm x 176cm) = 665,984 k cals = 86.39 kg]
	
	Skeletal Weight = 12% Female body weight [12% BW x 665,984 k cals = 79,918.08 = ] 
		          15% Male bodyweight    [15% BW x 665,984 k cals = 99,897.6 = 12.96 kg ] Internals/Static
	   Organ weight = 25% of bodyweight      [25% BW x 665,984 k cals = 166,496 = 21.6 kg]  Internals/Static
	Base Fat = 28% of bodyweight           [28% BW x 665,984 k cals = 186,475.52 = 24.19 kg] (3% Higher for women) Reserve
	Base Muscle = 30% of bodyweight       [30% BW x 665,984 k cals = 199,795.2 = 25.92 kg] Converted
        Base Fluid Comp = 2% of bodyweight     [2% BW x 665,984 k cals = 13,319.68 = 1.73 kg] Internals/Cannot exceed
	Base burn rate Ratio = 3:1 [Muscle:Fat] for every 3 muscle cals burned: 1 cal of fat is burned [(3/.017) = approx. 176.5 turns]
        
	BMI Formula= [Weight/(Height x Height)] x 10,000

							*Muscle Gain & Loss System*

				MUSCLE GAIN
	Triggered by: Caloric surplus + strenuous activity + high carry weight
	
	gain_modifier = (avg_daily_heavy_activity_kcal / 1000.0) + (avg_daily_carry_weight_kg)
	
	Hard cap: MUSCLE_CREATION_CAP_KCAL = 3500 kcal per day max muscle gain
	
	Logic:  Character must have surplus calories AND be performing heavy activity/carrying weight. 
	The surplus is converted to muscle up to the daily cap.
	Without activity stimulus, surplus goes to fat instead.

				MUSCLE LOSS
	Triggered by: Activity imbalance (sedentary > heavy) + moderate activity presence
	
	muscle_loss_factor = [avg_weekly_sedentary_minutes - avg_weekly_heavy_activity_minutes] × [avg_weekly_moderate_activity_minutes × 0.1]
	
	Logic: If character spends more time sedentary than doing heavy work, muscles atrophy.
	The presence of moderate activity slows atrophy (0.1 multiplier reduces loss).
	Pure sedentary (zero moderate activity) = maximum loss.
	Balanced or heavy-focused weeks = no loss or potential gain. 

				CALORIC CONVERSION
	Muscle mass stored as:  current_converted_value_ccv_kcal (3500 kcal = 1 kg muscle)
	Fat mass stored as: current_reserve_value_crv_kcal (7700 kcal = 1 kg fat)
	
	Deficit burn ratio: 3: 1 (Muscle: Fat) - muscles burned 3x faster than fat when in deficit

			DAILY vs WEEKLY PROCESSING
	Tick-level (short term: every hr): Handle immediate caloric balance (digestion vs burn)
	Daily: Calculate activity stimulus for muscle gain potential
	Weekly: Calculate activity pattern for muscle loss/atrophy

	BuildIndexValue:          Fat Mass  Jacked ~6-13%/14-20%   Athletic ~14-17%/~21-24%  Average ~18-24%/~25-32%   Obese ~26+%/~32%     	Essential Fat ~3-5%/~8-10%
			(Men/Women)

			Activity Thirst Rate -
	Resting In Heat - 2,541.67ml per hour-5.0 liters per hour in elite
	Average: Most people lose 0.5–2.0 liters per hour.
	Moderate Intensity: Roughly 1.0 liter (34 oz) per hour is common.
	High Intensity/Endurance: 1.5-2.0 liters per hour Rates can exceed 2,500 ml–3.0 liters per hour in elite

			Thirst-Lvls
	Mild Thirst (1%–2% Loss): This is the initial "thirst threshold".
	Strong Thirst (3%-4% Loss): Characterized by persistent, "very thirsty" feelings. Physical symptoms like dizziness, loss of appetite, and faintness often begin here.
	Extreme Thirst (5%–6% Loss): The urge to drink becomes overwhelming. This level is often accompanied by headaches, significant fatigue, and flushing of the skin.
	Severe Dehydration (10%+ Loss): thirst sensations may be overshadowed by life-threatening symptoms like delirium, seizures, and potential organ failure

			Thirst-Type
	Osmotic (Intracellular) Thirst: Triggered by ssalt and not enough water in your blood (e.g., after eating salty snacks).
	Hypovolemic (Extracellular) Thirst:  Triggered by a decrease in total blood volume

	The Satiety Signal: the brain "predicts" hydration and shuts off thirst signals within minutes of drinking. [Trigger signal to lower satiation Lvl on drinking before applying effects]

									Age
			
					Age-Bracket: Prime [16-35] [Effect: No-Accumulation] [Rate: 0 AFP/day]]
    					Age-Bracket: Middle-Age [36-55] [Effect: Accumulation-Starts] [Rate: 1 AFP/week]]
					Age-Bracket: Old [56-75] [Effect: Increased-Accumulation] [Rate: 1 AFP/day]]
					Age-Bracket: Venerable [76+] [Effect: Critical-Accumulation] [Rate: 5+ AFP/day (GM-Discretion)]]

								Cumulative Age Fatigue (CAF)
					Effect-of-AFP: For every [10 total AFP -> Penalty-Value: -1 Max-Vigor-Points (VP),  -1 Constitution [WillPow+END]
					Death-Condition: If Max VP = 0 [due to AFP accumulation], Death = Natural-Causes

									 Illness [Disease-Item]	
							Type: Viral, Bacterial
							Target_Species: Human, Animal, Plant 
							Transmission_Type: Airborne, BloodBorne, Contact, Foodborne, Waterborne 
							ID50 [InfDs]: The minimum load needed to establish infection
							Infection Rate (InfRt): How aggressively it spreads in a population [Float (e.g., 0.1 to 0.5)]
							Duration (Dur): How long a host is infectious (affects R0) [Time Unit (Turns/Hours/Days)]
							Target_BodyPart: Primary limbs/organs affected 
							Severity/Tier: A multiplier for damage/fatigue accumulation rates. Based Poisonsubtype Enums and #applied- +1 each

								Illness Tracking Variables [Character-sheet]
						These variables track the progression within an individual character.
						if an item animal or tile comes into contact with disease by appropriate method InfChnc is rolled *[roll or calc wil be used for CALCULATION]

							Infection_Load = 1
							Infection_Stage: Incubation, Infectious, Symptomatic, Recovering
							Time_Exposed: Total turns since initial exposure
							Immunity_Level: Character's acquired resistance to this specific pathogen strain 

							  Infection- Dmg Calc
					*Severity/Tier: Based Poisonsubtype Enums and #applied- +1 each
							Disease Progression [Dis_Prog] = [Severity x Infection_Load]/Toughness
							Excess_Fatigue_Accumulation [ExFAcc] = Base_Fatigue_Rate * [1 + [Severity/Stamina]]
							InfDs = log(Dis_Prog) + 0.5 - (ExFAcc / Target_BodyPart_Hp)
							Infection_Chance[InfChnc] = [ID50_Threshold/(Toughness + Resilience)] x Severity
							InfRt = (Infection_Load / InfDs) * Severity

		 					Illness Multiplier During Infection (Host_Growth)

						Viral Load: [viral RNA copies per mL = 133.3333 * e^((37.933 - Ct)/1.418)]
						Bacterial Growth Rate (k) (generations/unit time): Nt = Infection_Load * e^(InfRt * Dur)
			

							Spread [Reproduction Rate]
							Contact_Rate: Average number of unique interactions per [Time Unit].[integer]
							R0: The theoretical average new infections from one host.
								R0 = InfRt * Contact_Rate * Dur			
							Rt: Actual transmission potential at time (t).
								Rt = R0 * (Susceptible_N / Total_N)

						Illness_Recovery_Rate = 1(Infection_Load/ (Resistance)) x (1/(1 + (Time_Exposed/Dur))

		Resistances 
			Temp-Resistance Calcultion - Toughness + Resilience = %Temp-Resistance to Temperature change/Thermal Homeostasis Rate

			Temp->	Passive Normalization (The Drift)
				 Ambient Temperature (default 75 degrees F).

			    ->	The Drift Calculation:
				Drift = MAX(5, |CurrentTemp - AmbientTemp| / 50) × (1 / (1 + ExposureLength_Turns / NormalizationConstant = 9,000 turns (3 hours)))
				 [1 + ExposureLength_Turns = +1 skillpoint)

			Poison/CorrosionRes-> avg Cell turn over rate = 7 years (base)-> 2,555 days (x 3,500 kcal CREATION per day)-> 8,942,500 kcals (x Mass)(needed to BEGIN regrowing a Completey missing body part)
			Resistance = Abillity for cells to repair vs damage incurred, Reduces required kcal to resist decay
			
			Poison Potency Formula -LD50 = (ED50 / 3) * Wm * 10^-4 mg/kg
				ED50: The effective dose for 50% of the population.
				Wm: The individual's weight in grams.

			Corrosion Potency Formula -Corrosion Rate (mm/y) = 87.6 * (W / (D * A * T))
				W: Weight loss in milligrams., D: Material density in grams per cubic centimeter., A: Area of the sample in square centimeters.
				T: Time of exposure in hours., 87.6: A unit conversion constant.

			Poison_Damage_Per_Turn = (Poison_Potency / Target_Mass) × (1 - Target_Poison_Res%)
			Cell_Damage_Per_Turn = (Poison_Potency / Target_Mass) × Corrosion_Rate × (1 - Target_Poison_Res%) × Time_Exposed

			Edge Res, Impact Res = [(DMG ED/KD) recieved]/100
						DMG= Lifetime [only tracked after becoming Body Cultivator]

# --- SentienceComponent.gd (The N-P tag, attached to ANIMAL/HUMANOID/MONSTER entities) ---
extends Node

var is_sentient: bool = true
# Add logic for AI, movement, communication here

# Function to check role in grammar
func get_grammar_role() -> String:
    if is_sentient:
        return "N-P (Actor)"
    else:
        return "N-O (Object)"

# Function for state change on death
func on_death():
    is_sentient = false
    # Disable AI and movement scripts
    # The entity is now an N-O CORPSE

				Handling_Experience - 
Flat gain Rate (G) = 5

(M_tier)
Major Skill (3) = x1.20 exp gain
Minor Skill (3)	= x1.15 exp gain
Misc/Hobby  (3)	= x1.08 exp gain

Potential (P) = Skill Potential (Represents the character's innate theoretical application of a skill){Can be reduced to lvl 1 = 0 exp (capped min), Potential is increased with theorectical skill,Theorectical skill is always trained}[P = K_level - Φ_level]			
Knowledge  (K) = TheoreticalSkill(Represents the character's conceptual understading of a skill)[Caps proficiency][TheoreticalSkill_XP_Gain_Modifier = Aptitude * Potential_Multiplier{based on major and minor skill selection}][ΔK = G * Aptitude * M_tier]
Proficiency (Φ) = PraticalSkill (Represents the character's practical applibility of a skill)[As Prof. rises/ Potential falls][ProficiencySkill_XP_Gain_Modifier = Aptitude * TheoreticalSkill{based on major and minor skill selection}][ΔΦ = G * Aptitude * (1 + P)]

Potential Depletion = [PotentialLoss = Potential Exp - Proficiency Gained Exp][ΔP = ΔK - ΔΦ] 	
Exponential_Exp = [XP_Needed_For_Next_Level = Base_XP * (Level * Exponential_Factor)][XP_req = Base_XP * (n * E)]
Practical Skill Decay = P_Loss = Base_Decay_Rate * (1 - (Muscle_Memory_Score / 100))[ΔΦ_rust = -Base_Decay * (1 - (MM / 100))]



								Task Completion Time Calculation - " calculate - Skill effect on task"	
		
					1. TOTAL OBSERVED TIME (The Raw Baseline)
						T_{obs} = \sum_{i=1}^{n} s_i

					2. NORMAL TIME (Adjusting for Subject Skill/Performance)
						T_n = T_{obs} \times \left( \frac{R}{100} \right)

					3. STANDARD TIME (The Final Practical Estimate)
						T_s = T_n \times (1 + A)

							% WHERE:
					s_i = Time per individual step
					n   = Total number of steps (Task Complexity)

					R   = Performance Rating / Skill Factor (e.g., 100 = Standard)
					A   = Allowance Factor for fatigue/delays (e.g., 0.15 = 15%)

                 		The final formula to determine the subject's time to complete a task is:
					(T(s) = T(obs) x [R\100] x [1+A]
				Where: T(obs) is the sum of individual step-times.
					R is the Performance Rating 
					A is the Allowance Factor expressed as a decimal (e.g., 0.15 for 15%).

Breeding/Trait [Animals/Marriage]- [2 sets -1 from each parent. only one is rolled by Pc on char-creation][Spouses must sleep in same vincity/even if not in same party- For chance pregnancy roll = Capped at 3 times per week. {define roll chance, virilaty, fertility stat}  ]
1. Autosomes (Pairs 1–22)
These carry instructions for general body development and functions[affects Max lvl treshold]. 
Chromosome 1: Power = Strength + Dexterity = How much force the character generates
Chromosome 2: Accuracy = Perception + Dexterity = Charcters hand eye coordination skill
Chromosome 3: Charisma = Perception + Intellingence = Characters social awareness 
Chromosome 4: Stamina = Strength + Endurance = The amount of energy a character can exert at once 
Chromosome 5: Toughness = Willpower + Strength = How much damage a characters body can absorb
Chromosome 6: Quickness = Dexterity + Endurance = How well the character can navigate spacial movement
Chromosome 7: Resilience = Willpower + Percpetion = How well the character can guard against mental attacks &/or recover from them.
Chromosome 8: Muscle Memory = (Intelligence + Endurance + Dexterity)/1.5 = Governs skill retention and potential 
Chromosome 9: Aptitude = (Intelligence + Willpower + Perception)/1.5= How well the character can learn a skill, execute, and or strategize 
Chromosome 10: Constitution/Lifeforce [Qi/Ki/Chakra] = Willpower + Endurance = Represents the characters pysche and body (soul).
Chromosome 11: Metabolism - fat and Muscle threshold
Chromosome 23: Sex Chromosome

These carry instructions for Advantages-Disadvantages [Phenotype = Build, Appearance, Race, Genetic-Conditions, Genetic-Mutations]-  Can Slot = [Any chromosome with Effect]
Chromosome 12: Power = Can Slot [Power, Accuracy, Stamina, Toughness, Quickness, Muscle-Memory]
Chromosome 13: Accuracy = Can Slot [Power, Accuracy, Charisma, Quickness, Resilience, Muscle-Memory, Aptitude]
Chromosome 14: Charisma = Can Slot [Accuracy, Charisma, Resilience, Muscle-Memory, Aptitude]
Chromosome 15: Stamina = Can Slot [Power, Stamina, Toughness, Quickness, Muscle-Memory, Constitution]
Chromosome 16: Toughness = Can Slot [Power, Stamina, Toughness, Resilience, Aptitude, Constitution]
Chromosome 17: Quickness = Can Slot [Power, Accuracy, Stamina, Quickness, Muscle-Memory, Constitution]
Chromosome 18: Resilience = Can Slot [Accuracy, Charisma, Toughness, Resilience, Aptitude, Constitution]
Chromosome 19: Muscle Memory = Can Slot [Accuracy, Charisma, Quickness, Resilience, Muscle-Memory, Aptitude, Constitution]
Chromosome 20: Aptitude = Can Slot [Accuracy, Charisma, Toughness, Resilience, Muscle-Memory, Aptitude, Constitution]
Chromosome 21: Constitution/Lifeforce [Qi/Ki/Chakra] = Can Slot Stamina, Toughness, Quickness, Resilience, Muscle-Memory, Aptitude, Constitution]
Chromosome 22: Metabolism = Can Slot Any Chromosome and applies Effect (as is)[Chance slot for defect or mutation]

[Trait Rolling & Genetic-Mutations - For Pc/on char-creation Chromosome slots are filled in order [random or by player]. 
rule+ex. Chromosome 12: Power =  Can Slot [Power, Accuracy, Stamina, Toughness, Quickness, Muscle-Memory]
				 (Power)  [If slot has only matching "effect" -> No Mutation is rolled -> Take advantage/No disadvantage]
				 (Power + Con) [If slot filled with at least one matching "effect" -> No Mutation is rolled -> Take advantage/No disadvantage]
				 (Power + Accuracy) [If slot filled with matching "effect" & adjacent slot "effect" macth -> No Mutation is rolled -> Take advantage/No disadvantage/ +5% to adjacent slot stat](can be cancelled-out)
				 (Power + Stam) [If slot filled with 1 matching "effects" & 1 "can-fill" non adjacent slot -> No Mutation is rolled -> Take advantage/No disadvantage]				
				 (Accuracy + Stam) [If slot filled with adjacent slot "effect" macth & 1 "can-fill" non adjacent slot-> No Mutation is rolled -> Take advantage/No disadvantage/ +2% to adjacent slot stat]
				 (Stam + Charisma) [If slot filled with 1 "can-fill" non adjacent slot & "non-can-fill"-> No Mutation is rolled -> Take advantage & disadvantage]
				  -> If slot filled with 1 "can-fill" non adjacent slot & "non-can-fill"-> Next slot becomes adjacent slot to nearest "can-fill"											
				 (Charisma + Resilience ) [If slot filled with 2 "non-can-fill"-> Chance Mutation is rolled -> Take advantage & disadvantage]
				   -> If slot filled with 2 "non-can-fill"-> Next slot becomes adjacent slot to nearest "can-fill"
		if Power = Disadvantage-> If adjacent slot rolls disadvantage after rolling disadvantage-> Chance Mutation is rolled -> Both disadvantage become advantage]
		and Accuracy = Disadvantage
		Chance Mutations = Genes roll with _,_,_,or_ tags. If gene tag = natural state & "Chance Mutation" is rolled successful -> Mutation is summed/scored & stored (ex.+5% Power, +5% Constitution,=+10) until Chromosome 22 is rolled.
					-> After Chromosome 22 is rolled the "Chance Mutation" with the highest score checked for tag -> If trait = Dominant - trait is applied, Recessive - requires both parents
																			De-novo - Chance roll, X-Linked & male - apply (+Female for High Fantasy mode)
					->If first "Chance Mutation trait" ≠ Dominant, check for next trait until Chromosome 22 or dominant trait is found. 
					->If Dominant trait found, apply trait to Chromosome 22 (if from dfferent slot), and re-roll old slot. [Only applies Advantage/disadvantage & slot %. {Change slot rule not applied}]
					->If more than 1 Dominant trait found, apply highest score trait to Chromosome 22 (if from dfferent slot), and re-roll old slot.->Roll remaining mutations for proc-chance

Inheritance Type 	Probability if Both Parents "Carry"	Visible in Parent?
Autosomal Recessive	25% chance of condition			No (Carrier)
X-Linked Recessive	50% chance for sons			Usually No (Female)
Balanced Chromosomal	10–25%					No
			
			Probability De-novo
Spontaneous (De Novo):  (0.6% to 0.7%) 
Balanced Translocations: 10–25%  - for unstable version  


Dominant = (One copy required)
	Defacto Dominant =  LRP5 Duplication (Dense Bones), 15q11.2 Duplication (Hyper-Focused), Marfan Syndrome (Sky-Limb),
	Semi-Dominant = ACTN3 R-Allele (Fast-Twitch Dominant), MSTN Deletion (Extremely Muscled) (50% regular chance if dominant version) [can proc Dominant or Recessive]
	Dominant-De-Novo = Sotos Syndrome (Over-Bloomed), Malan Syndrome (Giant-Skull) [Can proc if Dominant or DeNovo]

Recessive = (Two copies required -1 from each parent) MSTN Deletion (Extremely Muscled), ACTN3 XX Genotype (Deficiency)

X Linked = Fragile X Syndrome (Fey-Face) [Male only]

De Novo = 47,XYY (Titan)(m), 47,XXX (Titaness)(f), Trisomy 21, 18, 13 (Small-Faced, Doomed, Broken),
	 Turner Syndrome (Half-Formed), 5p Deletion(Cri-du-Chat )(Developmentally Delayed),
	4p Deletion (Wolf-Hirschhorn) Distinctive Face Profile, Williams Syndrome (Honey-Tongued)[sporadic in vitro]

Uniparental Disomy (UD)= Two from one parent(Mixed)/Related Parents(Disadvantage)/One Parent=Chance[Balanced Translocations](Advantage)
			 14q UPD (Temple / Kagami-Ogata),Prader-Willi / Angelman Syndrome

Cognitive-Linguistic-trait: Language & Thoughtform are always determined by both parents


*LanguageParts:
		Idea: Moving-Part
		Action:	Prime-Mover
		Modifier: Something that Changes the shape of the Idea or Action

	Thought-Shape: Language is how ideas are expressed/what sounds represent
	  	
		E-Shape: All sounds combine to represent precise ideas
		W-Shape: Individual sound represent base things, and combine based on rules

	Thought-Order:
 	Isolated/Personal-
			Type_Base1: Idea
			Type_base2: Action
	  Familial/Cultural-
			Type_BaseA: Idea + Action	
			Type_BaseB: Action + Idea
	 Cultural/Regional-
			Type_1A: Action + Modifer + Idea
			Type_1B: Action + Idea + Modifer
			Type_2A: Idea + Modifer + Action
			Type_2B: Idea + Action + Modifer
			Type_3A: Modifer + Idea + Action		
			Type_3B: Modifer + Action + Idea


Cognitive-Linguistic-Gene: [orders combine[no change]], 
	combo orders have genetic chance to
		Type_A: 25% - Degrade [Remove a part from order],
		Type_B: 25%- Divide [Stay as dual orders ie. Type 1a + ype 2B],25% - Combine/collapse -> [Inherit one parent]/50% if both parents = Same parts different order/ 75% chance is same part same order”

Name-Types

Names&Language::
	Commonalities- [Languages share traits based on lvls of familiarity. Trade is what influences that dissapation.]
		Cultural:
		Regional: 
		Lingua-Franca: Languages: words/names that become common global lexicon through wide spread trade

	
	Differences- [Languages become more defined/distinct based on level of Socioeconomic function]

		Personal: Mix of Individual, Familial, and Cultural [Idiosyncracies]
		Familial: Based on Historic Socioeconomicstatus
		Cultural: Based on Historic Values/Traditions
		Regional: Based on Inter-Cutulral History [trade layer-> filters down]

	Phonetic_Profile:
		  Isolated/Personal: Specific and defined noise [#clicks, gluttal stops, emotive, yet unexpresive-literally unspoken]
		  Familial: Short often broken in full experssion [slang]
		  Cultural: Proper Most common speech that defines a Population
		  Regional: Commonalities of speech through observable shift {japanese,chinese}{latin,english}	

	Thought-Shape: Language is how ideas are expressed/what sounds represent
	  	
		E-Shape: All sounds combine to represent precise ideas
		W-Shape: Individual sound represent base things, and combine based on rules

	Shape-Sound:
		E-Sound: Singular, [Roman-Alphabet]
		W-Sound: Compound, [Romanized as Consanant/Vowel pairs or Double Vowels/Consanants]

	*LanguageParts:
		Idea: Moving-Part
		Action:	Prime-Mover
		Modifier: Something that Changes the shape of the Idea or Action

	BaseLanguageRule  [Profile-relation][Order of Thinking/output]
	Thought-Order:
 	Isolated/Personal-
			Type_Base1: Idea
			Type_base2: Action
	  Familial/Cultural-
			Type_BaseA: Idea + Action	
			Type_BaseB: Action + Idea
	 Cultural/Regional-
			Type_1A: Action + Modifer + Idea
			Type_1B: Action + Idea + Modifer
			Type_2A: Idea + Modifer + Action
			Type_2B: Idea + Action + Modifer
			Type_3A: Modifer + Idea + Action		
			Type_3B: Modifer + Action + Idea
	BaseNameRule:
			Characteristic:
				Observed/Desired 
					Single:
				 	 Compound: Specific/Literal [#ie.strong hands]
						    Relational	[m#ie. milk-white]
				
			Occupation: Word for specific occupation
			Ecological: for FN ecological names apply Modifier,for PN either Ecological type/ trait or both


							Currency:
						1 sila silver = 0.73 kg grain

							Conversion:
						1 gram of gold ≈ 12 grams of silver
						1 gram of silver ≈ 41 grams of copper 

						Inherent_Value_PreciousMetals:
				Silver: 1 gram silver ≈ 0.73 kg grain / (weight of 1 sila silver).
				Gold: Since 1g gold ≈ 12g silver, 1 gram of gold ≈ 12 × (0.066 kg grain) ≈ 0.79 kg grain.
				Copper: Since 1g silver ≈ 41g copper, 1 gram of copper ≈ 0.066 kg grain / 41 ≈ 0.0016 kg grain. 

 						ECONOMIC FORMULA: ITEM VALUATION
					var Currency
					var Currency_mass
					var Currency_material_type
					var labor_turns_taken: int             # Total turns spent creating item
					var worker_proficiency: float    # Proficiency (Phi) of the creator
					var market_scarcity: float       # Scarcity multiplier (Standard = 1.0)
					const BLU_PER_TURN = 0.0000055   # (0.132g Silver / 24000 turns) - Base Labor Unit

			func calculate_price():
    			# Material Cost (M)
    	var M = material_mass * material_type_val
    
   			 # Labor Cost (L)
    	var L = (labor_turns * BLU_PER_TURN) * (1.0 + worker_proficiency)
    
    			# Total Price (P)
    		var price_in_silver = (M + L) * market_scarcity
    return price_in_silver


			Suspicion= Suspicion of violating law or ethic, or of having  negative personality type
				General structure is Ingroup/outgroup = strong loyalty/suspicion of rival clans but is reversed for the Subversive (individual who counters the norm/inverses one oe mor collective principals/goals) where Ingroup/outgroup: suspicion of peers/strong loyalty to rival clans
																	Deceiptive (individual who hides subversive or deviant nautre)
																	Deviant (individual who's goal breaks taboo )
																	Liar (Pa = compelled to lie(habit))(So = to manipulate for gain)(Na = Lies for Ego)
																		(Co = Small lies)(Oc = Lies to not be left out)(Imp = lies with out rregard for long term)
																		(Av = lies to hide private details or avoid conseqence/reaction)(Pro = lies to protect others)
																	Suspicion lvl (instinctual supicion of person based on witnessed behaivor and known info. 
																		Suspicion represents that charachters chances of being a Subversive, Deceiptive, Deviant, Liar, Charlatan, or Infiltrator  )
																	Pessimist (individual who responds negatively to positive speech-type)
																	Optimist (Individual who repsonds positively to negative speech-type)
				
				Goal-structure is inverse. Individuals have complex-goals and simple methods. As the hierarchy moves up the goals-become simpler/focus and the methods more complex
					*Ingroup-outgroup - as hierarchry lvl rise suspicion between unknown in group memebers rise. ie (situation with no proof, and out of character (action does not equal habit)) 
								inter-family suspicion 5-10% for known family member if outof character (action does not equal habit) vs
								20-25% suspicion for unknown kin; however if fellow Statesman:  20-25% suspicion for known Statesman and no other association vs
								5-10% suspicion known Statesman and kinsman (implies/ clansman) vs  50-70% suspicion for known Statesman and unknown clan

Convo flow - 			1.Introduction: Choose Type:Pt1. Formal-> Greeting + Name [Assumed: Your's if theirs = Unknown, Theirs if = Known/ *Not for UEG/Enum tag]
(after Topic-Select)			 			      Informal-> Greeing Only
							      Pt2. Personal-> Char's"Default" greeting
								   Cultural-> Express appropriate formalities
									[When interacting with foriegn cultures, Cultural must be learned]
					 Initiator (Speech-Objective) vs Respondent (Set repsonse [Speech-Objective][start battle]/or AGREE [conversation resolves])
				2. Fight-> Initiator[ATTACKER] (ARGUMENT:[Rationale]+[Speech-Tone]+[Speech-Intent]+[Mood] -> Respondent[DEFENDER] (ARGUMENT: Rationale]+[Speech-Tone]+[Speech-Intent]+[Mood]) -> Dmg-Calc

					2-A. Rules-> Rationale: +1 Rationale-Type to act-> Tone: adds a (+),(-),(x2),or (0) to OPPONENTS-TONE->Intent: apply Opposition-Modifier

					2-B. Dmg-Calc-> Each party takes DMG corresponding to the Rationale-type  used against them, 
						If Rationale-Types directly oppose ie. Logos vs Logos only the difference in Dmg is dealt the weaker character.

		*[Npcs should have prefered Rationale-stat and auto to avoid regular-prolonged conversations, and early player-psyche drain.]

		*[Death-Battle: Convenant trigger an All or Nothing Argument. These Arguments cannot be quit by either party until all parties reach atleast -50% for each Rationale.
				 if either, main Attacker or Defender,quits the argument before resolution/outcome = NEGATIVE,
						->*Snapshot combat state and log to save, create dupe log memory.->]
							Everyday Char has chance to forget something from Combat log, forgetting any dmg taken will recover that dmg back to target Rationale-Stat
								Covenant option between Attacker and Defender Merge-logs and any Dmg that is "recalled" is reaplied to Rationale
									Last until whole combat-log is forgotten][if only one Party remebers only that Log is used and all remebered dealt Dmg is applied]
	
		Reaching-Cap: reaching a stat cap and using that action intiates "OVERKILL" 100% bonus but conversation ends. 
				[Overkill: any DMG over psyche limit is multiplied by disperity between Dmg dealt and limit by which cap was exceeded]

				RUMORS

		p_aware = witness_count/local_population
		p_unaware = 1.0 - p_aware
		H = -(p_aware * log2(p_aware) + p_unaware * log2(p_unaware)) else: H = 0
		freshness = 1/(1.0 + (turns_since_event / 72000.0))
		H_effective = H * freshness_mod
		base_decay = 0.01
		decay_rate = (1.0 - H_effective) * base_decay
		var rumor_id: int

Spell-Composition-Flow->
[Precomposed Always]Base-Spells = 1 Intent + Energy-type(+,-) + 1 Spell-type(single,continuous) + 1 Activation Method + 1 Spell-Nature = "Init Cast"
Primary-Spells-> [Quick-Cast = Precomposed] = Activation Methods(Additional/Reduce "Difficulty"/Increase Cast time [1 + turn per method w/out mag. mod]) + Spell-Natures (Additional) + Shaping + Modifiers[ETEM Magnitude, IntM Magnitude, NMR ->1. Magnitude (set as normal: All 9 effects set same Magnitude), 2.Removal (Adjust Magnitudes individually for each of the 9 nature-methods, or Remove (a) Nature-Method/(s)), Oscillation Rate] = "Focus Multipliers"
Aux-Spell - Primary Spell [Built from a Second or  Same Base-Spell][Activation Methods(Additional/Reduce "Difficulty"/Increase Cast time [1 + turn per method w/out mag. mod]) + Spell-Natures (Additional) + Shaping + Modifiers[ETEM Magnitude, IntM Magnitude, NMR ->1. Magnitude (set as normal: All 9 effects set same Magnitude), 2.Removal (Adjust Magnitudes individually for each of the 9 nature-methods, or Remove (a) Nature-Method/(s)), Oscillation Rate] + Modifier [On Cast, On Hit] = "Focus Multipliers"x2
Tertiary-Spell - [Same as Aux-Spell, but Tied to Aux-cast instead of Primary][Activation Methods(Additional/Reduce "Difficulty"/Increase Cast time [1 + turn per method w/out mag. mod]) + Spell-Natures (Additional) + Shaping + Modifiers[ETEM Magnitude, IntM Magnitude, NMR ->1. Magnitude (set as normal: All 9 effects set same Magnitude), 2.Removal (Adjust Magnitudes individually for each of the 9 nature-methods, or Remove (a) Nature-Method/(s)), Oscillation Rate] + Modifier [On Cast, On Hit] = "Focus Multipliers"x3

 Target tracking is done through Target Vectors where: Ground Vector: represents Target-Body-Position. Target Vector: represents Target-Body, where (0,0) equals Centerline-midpoint of the body

	Combat allows for as many move selections as the player wants since each has a time cost. A simple end turn button handles any issues. If weapon unsheated/fists up = Combat state
	Combat button = Armed/unarmed
	End turn = execute-perform loaded actions, 
	   	sheathe weapon/put fists down - ends combat, 
	   	Armed/Unarmed - change from fist to selected equipped weapon or vise versa 
[The ai can always calculate 2 moves, because interruptions allow for new selection.
*for Ai[Opposing Armies/Parties Avg = Mortal Enemy before any social modifiers are weighted. vs Mortal Enemy Behavior (Base)= will kill if legal]]
  
	Combat States- [Z axis position when not standing- Inflicted/Afflicted: Knocked Down [chartacter on ground], Inflicted: Afflicted: Low Float/ed [floating/falling between midpoint and ground lvl], Inflicted/Afflicted:High float/ed [floating/falling from mid-point or above],]
 
									 Hit-Chance & Evasion calc.-
	* Both are expressed as percentages out of a 100% chance. (a base characters Evasion of ([10(Acc)+10(Agile)] x .01 = .20 or a 20% Base evasion rate)
	* For the static combat calc [Hit-Chance]-[Evasion] = X if X = 0, there is no chance to dodge and damage is immediately calculated. *this calc is representative of 2 stationary combatants.
	* [Example of regular Hit-Evade calc before die roll for chance] = Attacker = [Hit-Chance + Spatial modifier]-[Evasion + Spatial modifier] = X,
                                                                   Attacker Advantage: If X > 0 the Attacker has an  H% [percent conversion [(1-X) x 100 = Y percent chance to hit]]. a 1d100 die is rolled and the number rolled (R) must be R <(Less than)/(or)=(equal to) Y to hit (go to damage calc)
								   Defender Advantage: If X < 0 the Defender has an D% [percent conversion 1a = [((-1) * X) x 100 = A] percent chance to chance to dodge]. a 1d100 die is rolled and the number rolled (R) must be R <(less than)/(or)=(equal to) A to dodge (skip damage calc)
								   
								 	Formula ,step 1 = [Attacker - Defender] = X, X = 0 (no advantage, calc dmg), X > 0 (Attacker advantage) , X < 0 (Defender Advantage)
										 step 2 =  Die roll for success or fail 
										 step 3 = After a failed advantage roll, a disadvantage roll is performed. (if Defender has adv. and fails to dodge, a roll for hit chance is initiated)
                                                                                           Disavntage formula [[(1s-X) x 100]-25% = Y] (R) must be R <(Less than)/(or)=(equal to) Y to hit (go to damage calc or skip is dodging)

	[Pc Action: Rest vs Meditate: Rest- a gen. action to recover stamina. (Gains bonus from sitting, sitting supported, sitting shaded(under canopy)/when applicable, Laying (infers supported bonus),surface comfort lvl )
				Meditate - gen action for ki-formation (confers rest status for Cultivators) - Action for Qigong (Breathe Control)- trains (Control Skills)[Skill name: Jitsu-Jutsu]]	


Combat_Prestige - Percieved Combat ranking. Base on Weapon Skills/Moves -> Combos -> Multistage moves. 
				Combos can be made freely, learned from others, or taught to those who want to learn, or learn through "Osmosis". 
					Combos Shared with others have shared prestige lvl (tracked through Dissappation method)
           		Prestige = Combat Score - Sum of all Combo Lvls [A combos prestige rating/stats only trained in actual battle against Npc and must have witness to move use Prestige gain - 
					For every hit/attack of combo landed x dmg of attack, all combos gain prestige on win  [Loser Prestige - Victor Prestige = Prestige earned for each combo if x = 0 or less than "no change"]/ 
				Prestige Loss - Whiffed [every hit/attack of combo missed x number of consecutive-attacks missed], all combos lose prestige on defeat 
							[Victor Prestige - Loser Prestige = Prestige earned for each combo if x = 0 or less than "no change"]
         
				Combo Stats = Stamina Cost- Stamina lost if Combo is completed flawlessy with no resistance
			 	 		School - Name of fighting Style. Must Name style if unique (Styles with shared names from seperate creators will share prestige)
			 			 Master - Leader of School (Faction)
			  			Creator - Character who made Combo

				Prestige lvl - [Higher than Tracked prestige] = Skill level -> This is the social representation of your skill stat. 
							It determines your percieved item/work quality, and influences you comes to you and why.

	Dual Nature: Transformation = [Acts as X Element(al-association) in reaction with Y element = If output and Magnitude =]/Chakra-Activation Type 1[Charka Point-Meridian Flow activation]

	Fire - 	Wood - Fuels Fire = Earth
		Earth - Fire refines Earth = Metal
		Metal - Fire melts Metal = Ice
		Ice - Fire Melts Ice = Water
		Water - Extinguishes Fire = Air
		Air - Strengthens Fire = Lightning
		Lighting - produces = Fire
 
	Water - Air - Water Cools in Air = Ice
		Ice - Water crystalizes into Ice = Metal
		Fire - Water extinguishes Fire = Earth
		Earth - Water is absorbed by Earth = Wood
		Wood - Water grows Wood = Lightning
		Lightning - Water conducts Lightning = Air
		Metal - Water reforms Metal = Fire 
	

	Air - 	Fire - Air consumed by Fire = Water
      		Water - Air cools Water = Ice
      		Ice - Air Strengthens Ice = Earth
		Earth - Air erodes Earth = Metal
		Metal - Air oSxidizes Metal  = Wood
		Wood - Air creates friction = Lightning
		Lightning - Air ignites with Lightning = Fire

	Earth - Lightning - Earth absorbs Lightning = Metal
		Metal - Metal in Earth forces out = Water
		Water - Earth absorbs Water = Wood
		Wood - Earth compresses Wood = Fire
		Fire - Earth smothers Fire = Air
		Air -  Earth transfers heat to Air = Ice
		Ice -  Earth deposits ion into Ice = Metal

Spell-Type (Cast-Consumption (Type/Modifier)) -		Single Cast - Once cast conditions are met, "MP" is consumed to cast and consumed portion is free to regen
[Is-Modifier][No Difficulty]							Continuous Cast - Once cast conditions are met, "MP" is consumed to cast. The spell is Continously cast ("held") until cast(selected) again/[turned off]. 
										The "MP" consumed to cast the spell remains depleted until the spell is "turned-off".

						No Contract Summons: 
							[Elemental-Nature:	[Summons: Clone [Mimic-Summon, Shadow-Summon, Mirror-Summon] or Elemental (Form: Humanoid or Wisp)
									1 - [Elementals: An Elemental does not need a Contract to be summoned. 
											[A "Marriage"/Joining Contract can be made with a Summoned Elemental for instant Mastery (All skills learned, bonus power to cast) of that Nature at the cost of being unable to use any other Elemental Nature-Magic.
												Under this contract the Elemental's Lifeforce(Vp), health(HP), and Stamina are merged [permanently.]
												This Contract is Single cast/Continuous meaning it is irreversible {even through causal-means}. This is the only Contract that can be made with an Elemental, and if Married to an Elemental it is the only Summonable Elemental.
												After Marriage to an Elemental, every skill-point gained in Summoning grants a chance to spawn "Children".
												Child: A child is an Elemental/Human Spirit hybrid that function as a Elemental & Clone. If Character Main Element = Elemental-element -> Child -Has same affinity and x2 power/skill(in that element) as the character/parents]
																							  If Character Main Element ≠ Elemental-element -> Child -Has Duel affinity and x1.5 power/skill(in a chosen element) from the character/parents]

												Elementals-Summoned (by Nature-Cast) - Water: Can Summon  Air & Water  
	    															       Fire: Can Summon Air & Fire
	    															       Air/Wind: Can Summon Air, Fire, & Water
	    															       Lightning: Can Summon  Air, Earth, Fire, & Water
            															       Earth: Can Summon Earth, Fire, & Water			
				 												       Wood: Can Summon	Air, Earth, & Water		
            			  												       Metal: Can Summon Air, Earth, & Fire,			
									
									2 - [Clone: Clones are made of the select Element but functionally have the same skill as the player[Pulse determines the # of copies made.]
											Summonable Clones are split into 3 types: Mimic, Shadow, Mirror
													Mimic-Clone: Mimic-Clones clones with no skills. Can resemble any thing/object the caster can mold. These are mainly used for quick subterfuge [distractions and substitutions][Functions as Counter/Reaction]
													Shadow-Clones:  A copy that possesses the user’s exact Body-Stats and Skills. Since Clone is copy of character Magnitude will determine Hp of Clone, with specific stats[denisty, volume] being set through the Nature-Modifiers. 
																Shadow Clones are capable of indepent operation and upon disperal break down into the element they are composed of. Futhermore the caster gains any aquired knowledge, and regains any VP unspent by the clone.
																	*NOTE: Ki pool (VP) is split between Shadow-Summons. Meaning 1 Shadow-summon = 50% ki for caster + 50% ki for S-s, 2 = 33.333% split and so on]
													Mirror-Clone: a specialized entity that acts as an extension of the user. The Mirror clone can act independently or mirror the casters movement. The Mirror Clone has its own Spell-set seperate from the caster. Health and stats are shared among the caster and Mirror clone
																*If Mirror-Clone is Summoned, a Contract is made and becomes the only Summon the Caster can call.]
					
						Contract - [(seal-section)- Contract seals function as a target-setter for the Contract-spell it self. The Spell-itself works through exchanging "Aether" between Caster and the Target, (Works like a magentic bond that can be turned on-off or weakened)]
							[Tether - Tethering is the "exchange of Aether" in Contracting, but in this sense it is used when the Caster-gives their Energy to an object and takes none from it. Tethering the "Contract" to that object alone.]

						Contract Summons: [Summons: Object-Summon (Bound, Unbound), Enity-Summons [People, Animals [Normal, Sage], Spirits, Monsters, Sentient-Objects]

								1 - Object-Summons: [Unbound-Object - Summoned directly by the catser through the "Contract"]
											[Bound-Object - Caster can apply the Contract for an object to another object. This removes the contract from the caster letting anyone who holds the bound-item and capable of summoning call the item.]

								2 - Enity-Summons: Enitity Summons are always summonable directly by the caster a but can be bound to items for multi-activation/summoning]	

						Conjure - Elemental-Nature determines the medium the object must be conjured through/from and the effect produce when Conjured. [ can either activate the effect or absorb and gain the proprties of the Element.(Difficulty determined by mass) ]

						Stregthen/Weaken - Effects Caster's control over the Selected nature and body-part connecte to that nature. [See Unified-Element Chart]

						Illusion - Creates Illusion and Ilusory effect of Element [alters mood]

						Percieve - Elemental-Nature Reveals Chakra-points and directly conntected body-part-info for Entities. For Objects shows stats linked to that Nature.						 - 

						Control - Allows for control over that element in associated target.

						Seal - [Protective - Protects from Opposing-Element attuned in Seal ie - Fire Seal protects Wood, is strengthened by air [see U-E chart]
							[Binding - Seals Nature or Connected body part
							[Tracking - Shares the input from connected body-part]
							[Contract - see Summons*]

						Displace - Attunes spell to move chosen Element [Every element of chosen target doesnt have to be chosen just a majority. ex sword - metal  or metal and wood would both suffice to be able to displace it. a Person = 7/7 Elements + Aether= 8 so atleast 5 of those categories would have to be selected to displace a person and "Metal" would need to be included to ensure refined items outside of Earth catergory ]

						Transmute - Sets Element to be Transmuted

						Barrier/Domain - Set Properties inside Barrier/Domain
						
						Container - Set Properties of container
						

Casting-Patterns (Shaping) - 				Type-Composition/Type-UseMethod	
[Focus only]			None - 			Spell is Cast Formless in open-air. If Cast on Self is Cast within the body	
				
				Projectile - 		[A Missle-Shaped object (Fires with Edge Horizontal)][FocusEffect = Mass(kg)= Length (m) + Width(m) + Height(m), Edge-Radius]
				
				Ray - 			[Line/Oscillation][ FocusEffect- dmg per sec = (Mass (kg) = Volume (m³) x Density (kg/ml))/Length(m)]
Modifiers:			    Beam - 		[Bundle of Parallel Rays/(Bigger Line)][FocusEffect-per sec of base Ray x # of rays]
Magnitude			    Parallel Beam - 	[Mulitple Parallel Beams][FocusEffect- dmg per sec of Each beam = Effect-per sec of base Beam /# of Beams]
				    Divergent Beam - 	[Cone- Diverges away from caster][FocusEffect-dmg per sec of Each beam = Effect-per sec of base Beam /# of Beams][Stronger closer to Caster]
				    Convergent Beam - 	[Cone- Converges away from caster][FocusEffect-dmg per sec of Each beam = Effect-per sec of base Beam x # of Beams][Stronger further from Caster]
				
				Orb -			[Barrier/ Hollow inside][FocusEffect = (Area(Hemisphere) = 4πr²)(m²)/Orbs created]
							[Container/ Dense inside][FocusEffect = (Mass (kg) = Volume((4/3)πr³)(m³) x Density (kg/m³))/Orbs created]
				
				Cube -			[Barrier/ Hollow inside][FocusEffect = (Area = 6 x (Length(m) x Width(m))(m²)/Cubes created]
							[Container/ Dense inside][FocusEffect = (Mass (kg) = Volume(Length x Width x Height)(m³) x Density(kg/m³))/Cubes created]
				
				Lune - 			[Crescent][FocusEffect of Hit = Area((2πRadius¹(m²)-2πRadius²(m²))²x(π))(m²) x (Mass = (Area x Length x Height(m³) x Density(kg/m³))/Number of projectiles = Float = 0.000 (return number should be no longer than)(r = radius(m))]
				[+2 Difficulty]

				Tetrahedron - 		[Pyramiadial (Deals all Physical-type dmg/Act as barrier or container)]
				[+2 Difficulty]		[FocusEffect of Barrier = (Area = Surface-Area((square-root of 3) x (EdgeLength (m))) x Volume(EdgeLength(m))/(6/(square-root of 2))(m²)/Tetrahedrons created]
							[FocusEffect of Container = (Mass(kg) of target = Volume (m³) x Density (kg/m³))/Tetrahedrons created]
				
				Domain - 		[+3 Difficulty]
				  [Tesseract]		[FocusEffect as Tesseract = (Area = 8 x (Length(m) x Width(m))(m²) x (Mass(kg) = Volume(Area x Height)(m³) x Density(kg/m³)) x (Edge Radius(mm)]
				  [Hypersphere] 		[FocusEffect as Hypersphere = (Area(Hemisphere) = (4πr²)(m²) x (Mass (kg) = Volume ((4/3)πr³)(m³) x Density (kg/m³))]
				  *[Barrier & Container]   [Only 1 domain can be shaped or cast at a time, and naturally have both the Container and barrier effect free of difficulty cost]

												*[Relativity Notes] - Controls the "Weight" of time. By increasing Density (Method 3), you create a gravity well that physically drags the passage of time into a crawl.]
							
							Space			[Position - Increase/Decrease Coordinate-Stability [Strengthen/Weaken Spatial-Anchoring/Location-Fixity][Effect]]

												*[Position Notes - Governs "Where" an object exists. High Fixity anchors an object to a coordinate, while Phase-Shift allows an object to bypass physical collisions by desyncing from local space.]

												*[Volume Notes - Governs "How much" space exists. By manipulating Area (Method 3), you can make a ten-foot hallway require a hundred feet of travel to cross.]

Dmg Type Calc -						[Hit/Impact = (Mass (kg) = Volume (m³) x Density (kg/m³))]

							[Hit/Pierce = (Edge Radius (mm) x (Mass (kg)]
							[Hit/Ray/Beam = ((Mass x Length)⁻²)(Duration⁻²)]



System - 

	Every Level of Control (skill)	the character gains grants 1 skill point. Skill points can be used to create base spells.

	Spell-Composition-Flow->[Cast Difficulty (= Init cast x Focus Multipliers)- Cast Cost = (Cast Difficulty x 10)] -> 1 Difficulty = 3,500 kcal
	[Precomposed Always]Base-Spells = 1 Intent + Energy-type(+,-) + 1 Spell-type(single,continuous) + 1 Activation Method + 1 Spell-Nature = "Init Cast"
	Primary-Spells-> [Quick-Cast = Precomposed] = Activation Methods(Additional/Reduce "Difficulty"/Increase Cast time [1 + turn per method w/out mag. mod]) + Spell-Natures (Additional) + Shaping + Modifiers[ETEM Magnitude, IntM Magnitude, NMR ->1. Magnitude (set as normal: All 9 effects set same Magnitude), 2.Removal (Adjust Magnitudes individually for each of the 9 nature-methods, or Remove (a) Nature-Method/(s)), Oscillation Rate] = "Focus Multipliers"
	Aux-Spell - Primary Spell [Built from a Second or  Same Base-Spell][Activation Methods(Additional/Reduce "Difficulty"/Increase Cast time [1 + turn per method w/out mag. mod]) + Spell-Natures (Additional) + Shaping + Modifiers[ETEM Magnitude, IntM Magnitude, NMR ->1. Magnitude (set as normal: All 9 effects set same Magnitude), 2.Removal (Adjust Magnitudes individually for each of the 9 nature-methods, or Remove (a) Nature-Method/(s)), Oscillation Rate] + Modifier [On Cast, On Hit] = "Focus Multipliers"x2
	Tertiary-Spell - [Same as Aux-Spell, but Tied to Aux-cast instead of Primary][Activation Methods(Additional/Reduce "Difficulty"/Increase Cast time [1 + turn per method w/out mag. mod]) + Spell-Natures (Additional) + Shaping + Modifiers[ETEM Magnitude, IntM Magnitude, NMR ->1. Magnitude (set as normal: All 9 effects set same Magnitude), 2.Removal (Adjust Magnitudes individually for each of the 9 nature-methods, or Remove (a) Nature-Method/(s)), Oscillation Rate] + Modifier [On Cast, On Hit] = "Focus Multipliers"x3

		Base-Spells - 	A Base spell consist of one Intent [Including Engery-Type Modifier], one Spell-Type , one Activation-Method, and one Spell-Nature = Inital Cast 
	
		Primary-Spells - Primary-spells are freely made from spells made from Base-spells and include all Focus effects to be applied to Base-Spell. Primary-spell components include any extra  Activation-Methods, or Spell-Natures. 
			This is also where cast-shapes and the shape modifiers are added to a spell. Primary-Spells can also function as Auxillary/Tertiary-Spells

		Auxillary-Spells - Auxillary-Spells can be freely created. Auxillary-Spells can be Simultaneous or Secondary, where Simultaneous-Spells activate at the same time as the Base-Spell
			Secondary-Spells activate after the Base-Spell completes its first activation.
		        Every component added to a Auxillary spell has x2 Difficulty.

		Tertiary-Spells - Tertiary-Spells are to Auxillary-Spells as Auxillary-Spells are to Base-Spells
		  Every component added to a Tertiary spell has x3 Difficulty

		Spell-Nature - Spell-Nature is essentially "How the spell works". Spell-Nature is seperated into 2-Categories & 3 parts, (ie...if one wanted to interact with a pure element; Base-Spell difficulty = 3 from Spell-Nature Alone.)
			Method consists of the mechanism by which that Nature function while Compostion consists of Pressure, the Force generated by the Nature, and Vibration, the physically manifested effect of the Nature.



Spell-Composition - 
(Cast-Difficulty and Cast-Cost)]
[Difficulty = Init cast x Focus Multipliers)] 
[Cost = (Cast Difficulty x 10)]

Spell-Utility & Combat

note*: All spells can created freely as long as the component is known. Spells can be created Theorectically [Directly in "Spellbook"] or Practically [Saved to "Spellbook" after casting]
       Any spell created Practically that is not from a Base-Spell will be treated as a Base-Spell with Auxillary-Spell-Difficulty. 
	Any spell created Theorectically that is not from a Base-Spell will be treated as a Base-Spell with Tertiary-Spell-Difficulty

			Tile-Size
	tile_size: Vector2 = Vector2(32, 16), = 1 Square meter
							  

		 # --- TIME CONSTANTS (1 game turn = 1.2 sec) ---
	var total_turns_passed: int = 0
	const TURN_DURATION_REAL_SECONDS: float = 1.2
	const TURNS_PER_MINUTE: int = 50 
	const TURNS_PER_HOUR: int = 3000
	const TURNS_PER_DAY: int = 72000
	const TURNS_PER_WEEK: int = TURNS_PER_DAY * 7      # 504,000 turns
	const TURNS_PER_2_WEEKS: int = TURNS_PER_WEEK * 2 # 1,008,000 turns
	const TURNS_PER_MONTH: int = TURNS_PER_DAY * 30    # 2,160,000 turns

	(in game day 12 am- 11:59/12am, game cycle (daily updates) 5am)

	World design note: Z-layer 6 tiles vertical. (Z0) 2 for ground lvl, and jumpable height. (Z1) 2 for underground storage/housing. (Z2)2 high for any levitation/flight effects that have 

	Map Total Dimensions Width: \(192\text{\ tiles}\times 32\text{\ px}=\mathbf{6,144}\text{\ pixels}\)Height: \(192\text{\ tiles}\times 16\text{\ px}=\mathbf{3,072}\text{\ pixels}\) 
	
	The World Hierarchical Scale
	Active (Embark) Tile: The smallest unit where actual characters and items exist.
	Local Block: A 48 x 48 cluster of active tiles.
	Region Tile: A 16 x 16 cluster of Local Blocks. This means one Region Tile contains 768 x 768 individual active tiles. 


WORLD SCALE HIERARCHY (Total Area: ~60,000,000 sq km)

1. GLOBAL (The Atlas Layer)
   - Scale: 1 Tile = 500km x 500km
   - Grid Size: ~16 x 16 Tiles
   - Contents: Continents, Oceans, Hemispheres, Biomes, Mountain Ranges,

GLOBAL_MAP GEN/COLORS-> tiles are populated by 4x4 colors, mixed areas = Ecotone/transition area
Part_1: 
	DEPTHS: Dark Blue: Represents the deepest water (abyssal plains and ocean trenches).
	-> Gen one Ocean -> break into 10 plates (5 subduction/Basalt plates, 5 rising/Granite plates) -> set MIDDLE_MOST_PLATE direction East -> (No adjacent plate can have same direction.)
			    -> at Subduction_Zone where Granite and Basalt meet Land_tile +1 all adjacent direction +1 height to current tile-> growth dissapates outward after initial 
					Land_tile +1  to all adjacent tiles and +1 height to all adjacent tiles & current tile
			COLLISION_MAP: 	2 GRANITE_PLATES fuse at a +2 height rate as -1 land creation occurs, if Tile/peak is +9 distribute + 1 height to lowest adjacent tile.
SHALLOWS: Light Blue: Represents shallow water, continental shelves, or areas near the coastline.
	
	
	BIOME GEN - CLIMATE MAP
			HEAT_CLIMATE_MAP_Cause: [BaseTile_HeatScore = ([GlobalTerrainTile_Height (x) -1]+ 10)]
						+ [BaseEquator_HeatScore = -> 10 (#max heat) (x) 12.10], where x = static, y = Drift Rate= sin(decant degree)/current time				
				+					Seasonal_Heat_Focus = Midpoint_Y + (sin(Current_Time * DR) * Max_Drift_Distance) Max_Drift_Distance = 15
			WIND_CLIMATE_MAP: = Tiles over 10 HEAT dipserse 1 heat to coldest neighbor until Tile_HeatScore = BaseTile_HeatScore, everytime a tile disperses heat increase its Wind_Score +1
						Wind_Score increases Heat disperse +1 per score and dispersal range +1 [so Wind_Score +2 adds +3heat to coldest tile (C) adjacent to the coldest tile (B) touching the current tile (A) ] 
							if gains HEAT + 1 decrease tile WIND_SCORE + 1 -> If  tile WIND_SCORE = -1 add +2 Heat to tile
				=
			MOISTURE_CLIMATE_MAP: Water tiles add 1 Water_Content to adjacent tiles during HEAT_MOVEMENT (Wind_Climate_Map).
				+		If Moisture_Content -> [Water_Content + Tile_HeatScore] ≥ 20 -> Water_Content = Rainfall_TypeA
			HEAT_CLIMATE_MAP	Rainfall_TypeA dipserse 2 heat & 1 Water_Content to coldest neighbor until Tile_HeatScore = BaseTile_HeatScore 
						Adjacent Tiles to Rainfall_TypeA tiles recieve Rainfall_TypeB = dipserse 1 heat & .5 Water_Content to coldest neighbor until Tile_HeatScore = BaseTile_HeatScore ->
				=			if Rainfall_TypeA is not triggered -> Rainfall on tile triggers Liquid_Height +1 & accumulates every turn until Rainfall ceases -> 
								if tile A has Liquid_Height +1 -> & Adjacent tile B GlobalTerrainTile_Height is Lower Water moves from tile A to B
												-> & Adjacent tile B GlobalTerrainTile_Height is same look for Lower tile	
													-> & Adjacent tile B GlobalTerrainTile_Height is same & no Lower tile -> if tile A Liquid_Height +2 move +1 Liquid from tile A to B if B = empty
														if tile A has Liquid_Height +2 or more -> & Adjacent tile B GlobalTerrainTile_Height is same & no Lower tile or empty tile B
														-> if tile B = Liquid_Height +1 & tile C = Liquid_Height +2 -> Move +1 Liquid from tile A to C 
															-> if Liquid_Height exceeds +3 disperse +1 to all adjcent tiles, & reduce GlobalTerrainTile_Height -1-> restart collection ->once all rivers have outlets = Waterway_Map 	
			AVGRAINFALL_CLIMATE_MAP: After waterway gen, rain map is passed over water map = FLOODPLAIN_CLIMATE_MAP -> Where any tile that collects +3 water = Bedrock, & 
				+														FERTILE Active Flood + Moderate/High Heat.
			WATERWAY_WORLD_MAP													CLAY	High Rainfall + No Flood + Low Drainage.			
																		LOAMY	Moderate Rainfall + Moderate Heat	
																		SANDY	Low Rainfall + High Heat

 
WATER-BODIES: Blue/Cyan: Indicates mid-depth water and larger inland bodies.
	[LAKES,WATERWAYS ]	


LOWLANDS: Denotes lowlands and plains (altitudes near 0–200 meters). Even a desert like the Mojave may be dark green if it is at a low elevation.
	[PLAINS, VALLEY, DUNE, BASIN, COASTAL PLAIN, WETLANDS (SWAMP, MARSH, FOG,BEN), SHORE, RIVERBANK]
RISING TERRIAN: Light Green: Represents low hills or rising terrain (roughly 200–500 meters).
HIGHLANDS/PLATUEAS: Yellow/Tan: Indicates plateaus or mid-height hills (500–1,000 meters).
	[HILLS,PLATEU, MESA, BUTTE]
MOUNTIAN/PEAK: Brown/Red-Brown: Represents mountainous regions (1,000–3,000 meters); darker browns indicate higher ranges.
	[MOUNTAIN_RANGE, CLIFF, CANYON, PEAK,]
SNOW-FIELD/GLACIER: White: Denotes the highest peaks and permanent glaciers or snowfields (typically over 3,000 meters). 
	[SNOW CAPPED PEAKS, ICEFIELD, GLACIER]

GlobalTerrainTile_Height=


Terrain Type	Height Score (0-10)	Structural Purpose
DEPTHS		0.0 - 0.5		Absolute base elevation.
SHALLOWS	0.6 - 1.5		Transitional shelf.
LOWLAND		1.6 - 2.5		Low-lying,  flats.
HILLY		2.6 - 4.0		Primary low-land TRANSITION baseline.
HIGHLAND	3.0 - 5.0		Overlaps Plains/Valley
PLATEAU		2.0 - 6.0		High variance; .
MOUNTAIN	7.5 - 9.0		Significant vertical leap from Plains (Escarpment Trigger).
GLACIER		9.1 - 10.0		Maximum elevation ceiling. (Max vis height =9 [-1 since it starts at sea floor level or 0])

if Mountain+plains-> transition-Cliff/escaprment

CANOPY_HEIGHT_MAP:

# 1. CLIMATE HEIGHT RANGES (The Base Variable)
# Determined by [Water_Content + Heat_Score] interaction within the ClimateEnum.

[TROPICAL / SUBTROPICAL] 
- Requirement: [Water_Content + Heat_Score] ≥ 25
- Range: 22.0m - 35.0m (Subtropical leans toward lower bound; Tropical toward upper)
- 4x4 Render: High Density (12-16/16). Multi-layer sprite stacks (Understory + Emergent).

[TEMPERATE_HUMID / MEDITERRANEAN]
- Requirement: High Water_Content + Moderate/High Heat
- Range: 20.0m - 30.5m (Humid can spike to 40m+ in Coastal variants)
- 4x4 Render: High Density (10-14/16). Large crown Hardwood/Conifer sprites.

[TEMPERATE]
- Requirement: Moderate Water_Content + Moderate Heat
- Range: 15.0m - 25.0m
- 4x4 Render: Moderate Density (8-12/16). Balanced mix of deciduous/evergreen.

[ARID]
- Requirement: [WIND_SCORE = -1] + [Heat_Score > 10] (High Heat / Low Water)
- Range: 5.0m - 12.0m 
- 4x4 Render: Sparse/Bimodal (2-6/16). Clumped Succulent and Dry-Shrub sprites.

[ARCTIC]
- Requirement: [BaseTile_HeatScore] < 2 (Maximum Heat Sink)
- Range: 0.27m - 5.0m
- 4x4 Render: Ground-cover (Moss/Algae). Sparse, low-profile Taiga/Tundra sprites.

[AQUATIC]
- Requirement: [Liquid_Height] > 0
- Range: 0.0m - 5.0m (Submerged/Surface)
- 4x4 Render: Water-Fern/Algae sprites. Height is restricted by Depth/Shallows score.


# 2. HEMISPHERIC DRIFT MODIFIERS (The Scaling Rule)
# Uses [BaseEquator_HeatScore] and [Latitude] to apply quadratic variance.

[SOUTHERN_HEMISPHERE] (Latitude < 0)
- Rule: Strong Latitudinal Dependence (R² = 67.1%)
- Calculation: Final_Height = Base_Height * (1.0 - (Latitude^2))
- Result: Predictable, sharp decline in canopy height as you move toward the South Pole.

[NORTHERN_HEMISPHERE] (Latitude > 0)
- Rule: Localized Climate Relationship (R² = 35.3%)
- Calculation: Final_Height = Base_Height * (0.67 + (Local_Moisture_Modifier * 0.33))
- Result: Greater variance; local "Heat Pockets" (like Mediterranean zones) can maintain height despite higher latitude.

3. LOCAL (The Playable World - YOUR BASE UNIT)
   - Scale: 1 Tile = 1km x 1km
   - Grid Size: ~7,746 x 7,746 Tiles (Totaling ~60M Tiles)
   - Contents: Cities, Villages, Landmarks, Supply Line Paths (Roads [DIRT/STONE]),
	SETTLEMENT RULES

 SETTLEMENT
   - Requirement: 1-9 Dwellings

 VILLAGE 
   - Requirement: 10 Dwellings

 TOWN
   - Requirement: 3 Villages (30 Dwellings total)

 CITY
   - Requirement: 2-3 Towns (60-90 Dwellings total)

SUPPLYLINE_TYPES:
	DIRT_TRACK
	COBBLE_WAY Requires LITHIC [SILICATE] 
	AQUATIC_ROUTE


4. PARCEL/SUB-TILE (The Detail Layer)
   - Scale: 1 Tile = 1m  (Dwarf Fortress/COQ style)
   - Grid Size: 500 x 500 to 1000 x 1000 per LOCAL tile
   - Contents: Buildings, Rooms, Specific Crops, Furnishings, Units

Summary Table for Tweaking
Property		Raising (↑) makes it...			Lowering (↓) makes it...
Density			Harder to move, sinks.			Lighter, floats, easy to throw.
Specific Heat		Slow to heat/cool (Stable).		Fast to heat/cool (Volatile).
Fusion Heat		Hard to liquify (Heat resistant).	Easy to melt (Flash-melt).
Vapor Heat		Stable liquid (Safe storage).		Easy to gasify (Inhalable).

#Material_Type

extends Resource

class_name Material_Type

@export var material_name: String
# Dictionary of chemical symbols and percentages/proportions (e.g., {"Cu": 0.88, "Sn": 0.12})
@export var elemental_composition: Dictionary
@export var description:  String
@export var dimension_length:  float
@export var dimension_width:  float
@export var dimension_height:  float

@export var ItemMiscCategory_type: Array [ItemEnums.ItemMiscCategory]
@export var material_type: Array [Material_Type] # Reference to a Material resource
@export var parts: Array [EnumsList.ItemTypeSubCategory]
@export var icon: Array [Texture2D]
@export var mass: float # Base mass of this specific shape (in kg)

# Function to retrieve stats based on the SubCategory Enum value
func get_stats_for_armortype_subcategory(subcategory_enum_value: ItemEnums.ItemTypeSubCategory) -> Dictionary:
	# We check if the dictionary has the provided enum value as a key
	if ITEM_ARMOR_STATS.has(subcategory_enum_value):
		return ITEM_ARMOR_STATS[subcategory_enum_value]
	
	# Return an empty dictionary if the subcategory isn't found
	return {}

enum Plant_Type {
    	HERB,       // Short plants with soft, green stems
    	SHRUB,      // Medium woody plants with multiple branches
    	TREE,       // Tall plants with a single woody trunk
    	CLIMBER,    // Plants requiring support to grow vertically
    	CREEPER,    // Plants with fragile stems that grow along the ground
    	GRASS       // Graminoids with hollow or flat stems
};

    EXTRACT,        // Concentrated substances (oils, resins)

    BIOMASS         // General organic matter used for fuel or compost

### 4C. Trait Types (Examples)
- GrowthTime: FAST, MEDIUM, SLOW
- DiseaseResistance: RESISTANT, PARTIAL, SUSCEPTIBLE
- StressTolerance, DecayRate: [0.0 - 1.0] float, sometimes enum for types (HEAT, COLD, DROUGHT...)
- ClimatePreference: TROPICAL, TEMPERATE, ARID, ARCTIC, AQUATIC
- SeasonTolerance: SPRING, SUMMER, AUTUMN, WINTER
- TerrainPreference: FOREST, GRASSLAND, MOUNTAIN, DESERT, WETLAND, COASTAL, UNDERGROUND
- ReproductionType: SEED, CUTTING, TUBER, BULB, SPORE, GRAFTING, LAYERING
- PollinationType: SELF, CROSS, WIND, INSECT, BIRD
- WaterNeed: LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH
- SoilPreference: SANDY, LOAMY, CLAY, ROCKY, FERTILE
- LightNeed: SHADE, PARTIAL, FULL
- Temperament: DOCILE, NEUTRAL, AGGRESSIVE, SKITTISH
- Pack/HerdBehavior: SOLITARY, PAIR, SMALL_GROUP, HERD, SWARM
- ActivityCycle: DIURNAL, NOCTURNAL, CREPUSCULAR, CATHEMERAL
